WEB RESEARCH RESULTS
----------------------------------------

--- Research Result 1 ---
Anomaly detection in long-term surveillance video is a rapidly evolving field with increasing importance for security, safety, and operational efficiency across various sectors. [scitepress](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-0) [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1) Research focuses on developing robust and accurate systems that can automatically identify unusual events in real-time, reducing reliance on human monitoring. [forasoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-2) [scitepress](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-0) Several key aspects and recent advancements in this area are highlighted below:

**Key Trends and Advancements:**

*   **AI-Powered Systems:** Modern AI video systems are changing how spaces are kept safe by spotting odd behavior faster than human eyes and saving money. [forasoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-2) These systems enhance threat detection capabilities and enable real-time monitoring of multiple feeds simultaneously. [forasoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-2) AI-powered anomaly detection systems can identify and respond to security incidents faster than traditional systems. [forasoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-2)
*   **Deep Learning Models:** Deep learning models, particularly Convolutional Neural Networks (CNNs) and Recurrent Neural Networks (RNNs), are widely used for feature extraction and temporal context modeling. [slogix](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-3) CNNs capture spatial patterns in images, while RNNs (especially LSTMs) model temporal dependencies between frames. [slogix](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-3) Hybrid models combining CNNs and RNNs leverage both spatial and temporal information for enhanced anomaly detection, achieving high classification accuracies. [forasoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-4)
*   **Unsupervised and Weakly Supervised Learning:** Addressing the challenge of limited labeled data, unsupervised and weakly supervised learning techniques are gaining traction. These methods train models on mostly normal activity, flagging deviations as anomalies. [mdpi](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-5) Federated weakly supervised video anomaly detection represents a significant advancement in privacy-preserving collaborative learning, enabling distributed clients to train anomaly detectors using only video-level annotations. [paperswithcode](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-6)
*   **Real-time Processing:** Enhanced real-time video surveillance systems with robust change detection and hybrid anomaly detection methodologies are being developed. These systems often use YOLO models for object detection (e.g., hidden faces, weapons) combined with RNNs for temporal analysis, achieving high accuracy in detecting novel anomalies. [researchgate](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-7)
*   **Privacy-Preserving Techniques:** Privacy is a significant concern in video surveillance. Approaches like PoseLift offer pose sequence data instead of raw pixel-level video, capturing human-body movements in abstract representations to ensure privacy. [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-8)

**Datasets:**

*   **Existing Datasets:** Several publicly available datasets are used for testing and benchmarking VAD models, including:
    *   UCF-Crime [paperswithcode](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-6) [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-8)
    *   ShanghaiTech [paperswithcode](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-6) [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-9) [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1)
    *   CUHK Avenue [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1) [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-9) [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-10)
    *   UCSD Peds2 [paperswithcode](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-6) [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1)
    *   VADD [paperswithcode](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-6) [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-11) [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-9)
    *   CamNuvem Dataset: A robbery dataset for video anomaly detection.
*   **MSAD (Multi-Scenario Anomaly Detection) Dataset:** A new dataset comprising 14 distinct scenarios captured from various camera views. [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-9) [openreview](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-12) [mdpi](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-5) It includes diverse motion patterns and challenging variations, such as different lighting and weather conditions. [openreview](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-12) [mdpi](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-5) [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-9) The dataset includes longer videos that capture the long-term evolution of video signals as well as anomalies. [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-9)
*   **PoseLift:** A privacy-preserving dataset specifically designed for shoplifting detection, containing anonymized human pose data from real-world scenarios. [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-8)

**Challenges and Future Directions:**

*   **Data Scarcity:** The limited availability of labeled anomaly data remains a significant challenge.
*   **Generalization:** Ensuring models generalize well across diverse scenarios and environments is crucial.
*   **Complex Environments:** Handling complex, real-world environments with multiple factors influencing behavior is an ongoing area of research.
*   **Integration of Multimodal Data:** Combining video data with other data sources, such as audio or text, can improve anomaly detection performance.
*   **Ethical Considerations:** Addressing privacy concerns and potential biases in surveillance systems is essential.

**Specific Techniques and Models:**

*   **YOLOv8 and CNNs:** Hybrid models integrating YOLOv8 for object detection and CNNs for classification are used for real-time accident detection and vehicle identification. [scitepress](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-0)
*   **Convolutional Autoencoders (CAEs):** Used for feature extraction and reconstruction, with anomalies detected based on reconstruction errors. [slogix](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-3)
*   **Graph Convolutional Networks (GCNs):** Improve anomaly detection by modeling spatial and temporal relationships between objects in crowded scenes. [forasoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-4)

**Real-World Applications:**

*   **Retail Security:** Detecting shoplifting and suspicious behavior.
*   **Traffic Monitoring:** Identifying traffic accidents and unusual traffic patterns.
*   **Healthcare:** Monitoring patient activities to detect falls or wandering patients. [scitepress](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-0)
*   **Industrial Safety:** Monitoring industrial environments for safety violations and equipment malfunctions.

In summary, anomaly detection in long-term surveillance video is advancing through the development of sophisticated AI and deep learning models, the creation of new and diverse datasets, and a growing focus on real-time processing and privacy-preserving techniques. These advancements are driving improvements in security, safety, and operational efficiency across various domains. [scitepress](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-0) [forasoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-2)


--- Research Result 2 ---
Anomaly detection in long-term video surveillance is a critical task with applications in public safety, security, and various monitoring domains. [mdpi](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-0) It involves identifying unusual events or activities that deviate from normal patterns in video sequences. [paperswithcode](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-1) [paperswithcode](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-2) [mdpi](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-0) [campussafetymagazine](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-3) [aip](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-4) Here's a summary of recent advancements and key aspects of this field based on the provided search results:

**1. [controlex](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-5) Core Concepts and Goals:**

*   The primary goal of anomaly detection systems is to promptly signal activities that deviate from normal patterns and pinpoint the time frame in which the anomaly occurs. [paperswithcode](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-1) [paperswithcode](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-2) [peerj](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-6) This is considered a fundamental aspect of video understanding, filtering out anomalies from typical events. [peerj](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-6)
*   Anomaly detection helps automate video surveillance by alleviating the need for constant human monitoring, saving time and resources. [mdpi](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-0) [peerj](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-6)

**2. [paperswithcode](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-7) [controlex](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-5) [mdpi](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-0) Datasets and Benchmarks:**

*   Several datasets are used for training and evaluating anomaly detection models, including:
    *   ShanghaiTech [paperswithcode](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-2) [openreview](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-8)
    *   UCF-Crime [paperswithcode](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-7) [paperswithcode](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-2) [paperswithcode](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-1)
    *   XD-Violence [paperswithcode](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-7) [paperswithcode](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-2) [paperswithcode](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-1)

**3. Approaches and Techniques:**

*   **AI-powered systems:** AI-driven security features are revolutionizing how security teams process and analyze vast amounts of video data, enabling real-time monitoring of multiple feeds simultaneously. [forasoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-10) [campussafetymagazine](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-3)
*   **Deep Learning:** Deep learning techniques, especially Convolutional Neural Networks (CNNs), have enabled significant improvements in object detection. [peerj](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-6) [mdpi](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-0)
*   **Anomaly-focused Temporal Sampler (ATS):** Integrates an anomaly scorer with a density-aware sampler to adaptively select frames based on anomaly scores, ensuring that the multimodal LLM concentrates on anomaly-rich regions, which significantly enhances both efficiency and accuracy. [github](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-11)
*   **Composite Recurrent Bi-Attention (CRBA) model:** Combines DenseNet201 for robust spatial feature extraction with BiLSTM networks that capture temporal dependencies across video frames, incorporating a multi-attention mechanism to focus on critical spatiotemporal regions. [mdpi](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-0)
*   **Spatiotemporal feature learning:** Integrating spatial and temporal feature learning is crucial for effectively capturing anomalies in videos. [mdpi](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-0)
*   **Use of Large Language Models (LLMs):**
    *   LLMs are being explored for video anomaly detection to leverage their reasoning and understanding capabilities.
    *   They can be used for tasks such as video anomaly question answering and providing explanations for detected anomalies.
    *   Techniques like semi-automated annotation engines that combine manual video segmentation with recursive free-text annotation using LLMs are being developed to create large-scale datasets for hierarchical video anomaly understanding. [github](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-11)
*   **Federated learning:** Federated weakly supervised video anomaly detection represents a significant advancement in privacy-preserving collaborative learning. [paperswithcode](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-2)

**4. Challenges and Future Directions:**

*   **Lack of comprehensive datasets:** The absence of comprehensive datasets with diverse scenarios remains a challenge. [openreview](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-8)
*   **Real-time processing:** Developing methods for real-time anomaly detection in video streams is an ongoing area of research.
*   **Complex scenarios:** Anomaly detection systems need to handle complex and diverse real-world scenarios, including variations in lighting, weather, and camera viewpoints.
*   **Ethical considerations:** Addressing privacy concerns and biases in AI models is crucial for the ethical deployment of AI-powered surveillance systems. [researchgate](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-12)
*   **Integration of spatial and temporal features:** Effectively capturing both spatial (where) and temporal (how things change over time) dimensions in video data remains a challenge. [mdpi](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-0)
*   **Evolving threats:** Surveillance products should remain cutting-edge and adaptable by implementing modular AI architectures, edge computing, and scalable storage solutions. [forasoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-10)

**General Challenges and Approaches:**

*   **Long-term tracking complexities:** Analyzing long-term surveillance video presents challenges because a person's appearance changes over time, and individuals may leave and re-enter the scene. [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0) [osf](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1) Face recognition can help reinitialize trackers, but it's not always available. (OSF, arXiv)
*   **Computational analysis:** Manual analysis of large amounts of surveillance video is difficult, motivating the development of computational analysis techniques. [osf](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1) (OSF)
*   **Slow-moving or stopped objects:** Handling slow-moving or stopped objects is a challenge for motion analysis and tracking in long-term scene monitoring. [andrewsenior](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) (Andrew Senior)
*   **Environmental factors:** Varying environmental conditions (lighting, weather), occlusions, and diverse human behaviors pose unique challenges for anomaly detection in surveillance camera data. [andrewsenior](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) (DiVA)

**Datasets and Benchmarks:**

*   **Need for long-term datasets:** Existing work often focuses on shorter video sequences (minute-long or hour-long). [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0) [osf](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1) (OSF, arXiv)
*   **TLP (Track Long and Prosper) Dataset:** A long video dataset for visual object tracking consisting of 50 HD videos from real-world scenarios, encompassing over 400 minutes (676K frames). [github](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-3) Each sequence tracks a single object. [github](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-3) A smaller TinyTLP dataset consisting of the first 600 frames of each TLP sequence is also available to highlight the challenges in long-term tracking. [github](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-3) (Abhinav Moudgil)
*   **LTFT (Long-Term Face Tracking):** A dataset conceived for multi-face tracking/detection in crowded scenarios, where the face is the only reliable feature for tracking. [paperswithcode](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-4) [paperswithcode](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-5) [paperswithcode](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-6) (Papers with Code, LTFT Dataset)
*   **UCVL:** A benchmark for crime surveillance video analysis with large models, including 1,829 videos and reorganized annotations from the UCF-Crime and UCF-Crime Annotation datasets. [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-7) (arXiv, PDF)
*   **SurveillanceVQA-589K:** A large open-ended video question answering benchmark tailored to the surveillance domain. [researchgate](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-8) The dataset comprises 589,380 QA pairs spanning 12 cognitively diverse question types, including temporal reasoning, causal inference, spatial understanding, and anomaly interpretation, across both normal and abnormal video scenarios. [researchgate](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-8) (ResearchGate) [researchgate](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-9)

[viratdata](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-10) (VIRAT Video Dataset) [viratdata](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-10)
*   **Multiview Extended Video with Activities (MEVA) dataset:** Features more than 250 hours of ground camera video, with additional resources such as UAV video and camera models. [viratdata](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-10) The dataset is designed for activity detection in multi-camera environments. [viratdata](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-10) (VIRAT Video Dataset) [viratdata](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-10)
*   **MOT16 & MOT17:** Datasets for multiple object tracking, containing indoor and outdoor scenes of public places with pedestrians. [paperswithcode](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-4) [paperswithcode](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-6) (Papers With Code)

Based on the search results, here's a summary of recent developments in anomaly detection in long-term surveillance video, focusing on papers published in 2023-2024:

**General Trends and Challenges:**

*   **Deep Learning Dominance:** Deep learning techniques, especially CNNs, Vision Transformers (ViTs), and LSTMs, are increasingly used for video anomaly detection (VAD) due to their ability to learn complex patterns from large datasets ([1], [2]). [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0) Hybrid architectures combining CNNs and LSTMs are effective in capturing both short-term and long-range temporal dependencies in surveillance footage ([1]). [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0)
*   **Evolving Research:** Research is expanding beyond traditional supervised learning to include weakly supervised, self-supervised, and unsupervised approaches ([1], [6]). [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0) [researchgate](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-1)
*   **Importance of Datasets:** The performance of VAD models heavily relies on the quality and diversity of training datasets ([3], [7], [12]). [neurips](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2) [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-3) [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-4) A key challenge is the lack of comprehensive datasets with diverse scenarios and the need for datasets that incorporate long-term temporal information ([3], [1]).
*   **Real-world Applications:** Anomaly detection in surveillance videos has significant applications in security, healthcare, traffic monitoring, and industrial monitoring ([1], [3]). [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-3) [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-4)
*   **Vision Language Models (VLMs):** VLMs are emerging as potent feature extractors for VAD, integrating visual data with textual descriptions to enable a more nuanced understanding of scenes ([1], [6]). [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0) [researchgate](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-1)

**Specific Papers and Datasets:**

*   **MSAD Dataset:** The "Multi-Scenario Anomaly Detection (MSAD)" dataset is a new dataset comprising 14 distinct scenarios captured from various camera views. [github](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-6) It contains 23,542 sentences, with an average length of 20 words, and its annotated videos are as long as 110.7 hours ([14]). [github](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-6)

[arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0) [researchgate](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-1) It investigates core challenges within VAD paradigms, including large-scale datasets, feature extraction, learning methods, loss functions, regularization, and anomaly score prediction ([1], [6]). [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0) [researchgate](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-1)

--- Research Result 5 ---
Okay, I will conduct targeted Google Searches to gather the most recent information on anomaly labeling methodologies used in recent long-term surveillance video datasets (2023-2024), focusing on datasets of the same scene across extended periods. I'm interested in how anomalies are defined, annotated, and validated in these datasets. I will then synthesize the information into a verifiable text artifact.

Based on the search results, here's a summary of anomaly labeling methodologies used in recent long-term surveillance video datasets (2023-2024), focusing on datasets of the same scene across extended periods:

**1. Definition of Anomalies:**

*   **Context-Dependent:** Anomalies are not always clearly defined and can be context-dependent. [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0) What is considered normal in one situation (e.g., walking on a sidewalk) might be abnormal in another (e.g., walking on a highway). [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0)
*   **Evolving Definitions:** The definition of anomalies can change over time, even for the same camera viewpoint. [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0) For example, anomalies during the daytime might differ from those at nighttime, or on weekdays versus weekends. [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0)
*   **Diversity:** Anomalies can range from subtle deviations to overt violations of normal behavior. [researchgate](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-1)
*   **Scene-Dependent:** Events that are normal in one scene can be abnormal in another. [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0)

**2. Annotation Methodologies:**

*   **Manual Annotation:** This involves human operators reviewing video footage to identify anomalies. It's accurate but time-consuming and not scalable for large datasets. [hitechdigital](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-2) The UCF-Crime dataset was manually annotated to create the UCA (UCF-Crime Annotation) dataset, containing 23,542 sentences with an average length of 20 words, and its annotated videos are as long as 110.7 hours. [github](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-3) [thecvf](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-4) [thecvf](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-5)
*   **Automated Detection:** Algorithms and machine learning models are used to identify anomalies in real-time. [hitechdigital](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-2) [scitepress](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-6) This is more efficient and scalable.
*   **Image-Level Anomaly Detection:** Analyzing entire frames to detect deviations from expected patterns based on the overall scene or context (e.g., unusual gatherings of people). [hitechdigital](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-2)
*   **Pixel-Level Anomaly Detection:** Detecting subtle anomalies like slight movements or changes in specific areas of a frame. [hitechdigital](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-2)
*   **Temporal Analysis:** Analyzing sequences of frames to capture motion patterns associated with anomalies. [scitepress](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-6)
*   **Multi-Modal Annotation:** Some datasets include annotations beyond visual data, such as textual descriptions of the anomalies. For example, the PreVAD dataset annotates each abnormal video with a text description, which has a total vocabulary size of 5,298 words and an average of 22.9 words per description. [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-7)

**3. Validation Methodologies:**

*   **Evaluation Metrics:** Establishing relevant benchmark evaluation metrics allows researchers to compare different methods and drive the development of better-performing algorithms. [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0)
*   **Cross-Dataset Validation:** Validating models on datasets different from the training data to assess generalization ability.
*   **Performance on Diverse Scenarios:** Evaluating model performance on different anomaly types independent of scenarios/contexts and on different scenarios independent of anomaly types. [openreview](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-8)
*   **Comparison with State-of-the-Art Models:** Comparing the performance of new models with existing models on benchmark datasets. [thecvf](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-5) [github](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-3)

**4. Datasets:**

Several datasets are mentioned in the search results, including:

*   **MSAD (Multi-Scenario Anomaly Detection):** A new dataset comprising 14 distinct scenarios captured from various camera views, with diverse motion patterns and challenging variations in lighting and weather conditions. [openreview](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-8) [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0) It includes 35 human-related anomalies and 20 non-human anomalies. [openreview](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-8)
*   **UCF-Crime:** A large-scale dataset of 128 hours of videos with 13 realistic anomalies.
*   **UCA (UCF-Crime Annotation):** A newly annotated version of the UCF-Crime dataset with fine-grained event content and timing, containing 23,542 sentences. [thecvf](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-4) [github](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-3) [thecvf](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-5)
*   **PreVAD:** A dataset featuring a hierarchical taxonomy of anomaly types and text descriptions for each abnormal video. [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-7)
*   **ShanghaiTech:** A dataset with frame-level and pixel-level ground truth for abnormal events.
*   **UCSD Anomaly Detection Dataset:** Features pedestrian walkways with anomalies like bikers and skaters.
*   **NWPU Campus:** Contains 43 scenes (camera views) to address scene-dependent anomalies. [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0)
*   **CUVA:** A large-scale benchmark for understanding the causation of video anomalies, with high-quality annotations. [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0)
*   **CHAD: Charlotte Anomaly Dataset:** A high-resolution, multi-camera dataset with bounding box, Re-ID, and pose annotations. [paperswithcode](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-9)
*   **LAD: Large-scale Anomaly Detection:** A database with 2000 video sequences and 14 anomaly categories. [paperswithcode](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-9)

**5. Challenges and Future Directions:**

*   **Lack of Unified Definition:** The absence of a unified and clear definition of anomalies. [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0)
*   **Data Scarcity:** The sporadic and rare occurrences of anomalies make collecting well-curated datasets difficult. [ijcai](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-10) [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0)
*   **Annotation Cost:** Laborious video annotation is a major reason why there aren't more large-scale VAD datasets. [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0)
*   **Generalizability:** Models often restrict themselves to detecting specific anomaly types and suffer from poor generalizability. [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0)
*   **Adaptability:** VAD systems need to adapt to evolving definitions of anomalies over time. [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0)
*   **Scalability:** Future studies should look into new ways to make anomaly detection systems more scalable and effective for large-scale video data. [ekb](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-11) [researchgate](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-1)
*   **Temporal Context:** Benchmark datasets should incorporate long-term temporal information to capture the dynamics of normal and abnormal behaviors accurately. [researchgate](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-1)
*   **Multi-Modal Data:** Integrating data from multiple modalities (visual, auditory, textual) can enhance anomaly detection performance. [researchgate](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-1)

**6. Techniques and Models:**

*   **Deep Learning:** CNNs, RNNs, and Vision Transformers (ViTs) have shown remarkable capabilities in learning complex patterns. [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-12)
*   **Few-Shot Learning:** Aims to adapt quickly to a new task with only a few training samples. [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0)
*   **Self-Supervised and Weakly Supervised Methods:** Used when labeled data is scarce. [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0)
*   **Vision-Language Models (VLMs):** Integrate visual data with textual descriptions for a nuanced understanding of scenes. [researchgate](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-1) [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-12)
*   **Gaussian Process Regression (GPR):** Used for video anomaly detection with localization and presentation of hierarchical features. [ekb](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-11)
*   **YOLOv8:** Used for real-time object detection in anomaly detection systems. [scitepress](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-6)
*   **LSTM:** Combined with CNNs for sequence learning in video classification. [scitepress](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-6)
*   **Hybrid Models:** Combining CNNs and RNNs to capture both spatial and temporal dependencies. [forasoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-13)
*   **Background Subtraction:** Identifying anomalies by learning robust background models and detecting deviations in foreground objects. [forasoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-13)
*   **Graph-Based Detection:** Using Graph Convolutional Networks (GCNs) to model spatial and temporal relationships between objects. [forasoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-13)
*   **Contrastive Learning:** Learning alignments between context, appearance, and motion to classify videos as normal or anomalous.

This information should provide a good overview of the anomaly labeling methodologies used in recent long-term surveillance video datasets.

Definition of Anomalies:**\n\n*   **Context-Dependent:** Anomalies are not always clearly defined and can be context-dependent. [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0) What is considered normal in one situation (e.g., walking on a sidewalk) might be abnormal in another (e.g., walking on a highway). [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0)\n*   **Evolving Definitions:** The definition of anomalies can change over time, even for the same camera viewpoint. [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0) For example, anomalies during the daytime might differ from those at nighttime, or on weekdays versus weekends. [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0)\n*   **Diversity:** Anomalies can range from subtle deviations to overt violations of normal behavior. [researchgate](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-1)\n*   **Scene-Dependent:** Events that are normal in one scene can be abnormal in another. [arxiv](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0)\n\n**2. Annotation Methodologies:**\n\n*   **Manual Annotation:** This involves human operators reviewing video footage to identify anomalies. It's accurate but time-consuming and not scalable for large datasets. [hitechdigital](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-2)\n*   **Pixel-Level Anomaly Detection:** Detecting subtle anomalies like slight movements or changes in specific areas of a frame. [hitechdigital](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-2)\n*   **Temporal Analysis:** Analyzing sequences of frames to capture motion patterns associated with anomalies.
